## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

        # RepoQA: Semantic Retrieval (SR-QA)

        ## Task: Find the Function

        You are searching a large codebase for a specific function based on its behavior.

        **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--8c9c67c0 (mirror of kubernetes/kubernetes)
        **Language**: go

        ## Function Description

        ```
        1. **Purpose**: Identifies which cluster nodes satisfy all scheduling filter plugins for a given workload, enabling the scheduler to narrow down placement candidates.
2. **Input**: Takes a context, a framework handle providing filter plugins and parallelism settings, cycle state, a pod specification, a diagnosis collector for recording filter failures, and a pre-fetched list of all node information objects.
3. **Output**: Returns a slice of node-info objects representing feasible placement targets, plus an error if any filter plugin returned a fatal error. Also populates the diagnosis object with per-node failure reasons as a side effect.
4. **Procedure**:
   - Computes the target number of feasible nodes to find, reducing to 1 if there are no extender filters and no scoring plugins.
   - If no filter plugins are registered, returns the first N nodes starting from a round-robin offset.
   - Otherwise, defines an inner closure that runs all filter plugins against each node in parallel, starting from the last scheduling cycle's offset to ensure fairness.
   - Uses atomic counters to track how many feasible nodes have been found; cancels the parallel search early once the target count is reached.
   - Records non-feasible node statuses into a result array under the parallel check, then copies them into the diagnosis object after all parallel work completes.
   - Measures and reports the total Filter extension point latency via deferred metrics emission.
        ```

        ## Search Strategy

        This function **cannot be found by searching for its name** because the name is not provided. You must:

        1. **Understand the behavior** described above
        2. **Search the codebase** to find functions matching this behavior
        3. **Explore the code** using call graphs and references
        4. **Narrow down** candidates until you find the exact function


        ## Output Format

        You MUST provide your answer as valid JSON and **SAVE IT TO A FILE**:

        ```json
        {
          "function_path": "path/to/file.ext",
          "function_name": "the_function_name",
          "justification": "Why this function matches: describe the behavior you found"
        }
        ```

        **CRITICAL**: You MUST save the JSON to `/app/solution.json`. This location is required for verification.

        **Your final step MUST be to run this exact bash command:**

        ```bash
        cat > /app/solution.json << 'JSONEOF'
        {
          "function_path": "ACTUAL_PATH",
          "function_name": "ACTUAL_NAME",
          "justification": "ACTUAL_JUSTIFICATION_TEXT"
        }
        JSONEOF
        ```

        ## Notes

        - The file path should be relative to repository root
        - Function names are case-sensitive
        - Provide your best match even if uncertain; explain your reasoning
        - The justification is scored on how well it explains the function's behavior

        ## Scoring

        - **Perfect** (1.0): Correct path AND name
        - **Good** (0.7-0.9): Correct path, similar name OR vice versa
        - **Partial** (0.3-0.6): Close approximation
        - **Incorrect** (0.0): Wrong function entirely

Perfect! I have successfully found and documented the function. Here's a summary:

## Solution Found

**Function Name**: `findNodesThatPassFilters`
**File Location**: `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go` (lines 629-712)

### Verification
This function matches all behavioral requirements:

1. **Purpose**: Identifies cluster nodes that satisfy all scheduling filter plugins
2. **Input Parameters**: 
   - Context
   - Framework handle (provides filter plugins & parallelism settings)
   - Cycle state
   - Pod specification
   - Diagnosis collector
   - Pre-fetched list of node information
3. **Output**: Returns slice of feasible node-info objects + error, populates diagnosis with per-node failures
4. **Implementation Details**:
   - Computes target feasible node count, reduces to 1 if no extenders/scoring
   - Returns first N nodes with round-robin offset if no filter plugins registered
   - Defines `checkNode` closure that runs filter plugins in parallel starting from last cycle's offset
   - Uses atomic counter `feasibleNodesLen` to track found nodes and cancel early once target reached
   - Records non-feasible statuses in result array, copies to diagnosis after parallel work
   - Defers metrics emission for Filter extension point latency

The solution has been saved to `/app/solution.json` as required.

\\treturn isAssumed\\n421: }\\n422: \\n423: // schedulePod tries to schedule the given pod to one of the nodes in the node list.\\n424: // If it succeeds, it will return the name of the node.\\n425: // If it fails, it will return a FitError with reasons.\\n426: func (sched *Scheduler) schedulePod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state fwk.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) (result nodes.\\n717: func (sched *Scheduler) numFeasibleNodesToFind(percentageOfNodesToScore *int32, numAllNodes int32) (numNodes int32) {\\n718: \\tif numAllNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\\n719: \\t\\treturn numAllNodes\\n720: \\t}\\n721: \\n722: \\t// Use profile percentageOfNodesToScore if it's set. err.(*framework.FitError)\n162: \t\tif !ok {\n163: \t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error selecting node for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n164: \t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, podInfo, fwk.AsStatus(err)\n165: \t\t}\n166: \n167: \t\t// SchedulePod() may have failed because the pod would not fit on any host, so we try to\n168: \t\t// preempt, with the expectation that the next time the pod is tried for scheduling it\n169: \t\t// will fit due to the preemption. It is also possible that a different pod will schedule\n170: \t\t// into the resources that were preempted, but this is harmless.\n171: \n172: \t\tif !schedFramework.HasPostFilterPlugins() {\n173: \t\t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"No PostFilter plugins are registered, so no preemption will be performed\")\n174: \t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, podInfo, fwk.NewStatus(fwk.Unschedulable).WithError(err)\n175: \t\t}\n176: \n177: \t\t// Run PostFilter plugins to attempt to make the pod schedulable in a future scheduling cycle.\n178: \t\tresult, status := schedFramework.RunPostFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod, fitError.Diagnosis.NodeToStatus)\n179: \t\tmsg := status.Message()\n180: \t\tfitError.Diagnosis.PostFilterMsg = msg\n181: \t\tif status.Code() == fwk.Error {\n182: \t\t\tutilruntime.HandleErrorWithContext(ctx, nil, \"Status after running PostFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n183: \t\t} else {\n184: \t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PostFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n185: \t\t}\n186: \n187: \t\tvar nominatingInfo *fwk.NominatingInfo\n188: \t\tif result != nil {\n189: \t\t\tnominatingInfo = result.NominatingInfo\n190: \t\t}\n191: \t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: nominatingInfo}, podInfo, fwk.NewStatus(fwk.Unschedulable).WithError(err)\n192: \t}\n193: \n194: \tmetrics.SchedulingAlgorithmLatency.Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n195: \t// Tell the cache to assume that a pod now is running on a given node, even though it hasn't been bound yet.\n196: \t// This allows us to keep scheduling without waiting on binding to occur.\n197: \tassumedPodInfo := podInfo.DeepCopy()\n198: \tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\n199: \t// assume modifies `assumedPod` by setting NodeName=scheduleResult.SuggestedHost\n200: \terr = sched.assume(logger, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n201: \tif err != nil {\n202: \t\t// This is most probably result of a BUG in retrying logic.\n203: \t\t// We report an error here so that pod scheduling can be retried.\n204: \t\t// This relies on the fact that Error will check if the pod has been bound\n205: \t\t// to a node and if so will not add it back to the unscheduled pods queue\n206: \t\t// (otherwise this would cause an infinite loop).\n207: \t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, fwk.AsStatus(err)\n208: \t}\n209: \n210: \t// Run the Reserve method of reserve plugins.\n211: \tif sts := schedFramework.RunReservePluginsReserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost); !sts.IsSuccess() {\n212: \t\t// trigger un-reserve to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n213: \t\tschedFramework.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n214: \t\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n215: \t\t\tutilruntime.HandleErrorWithContext(ctx, forgetErr, \"Scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n216: \t\t}\n217: \n218: \t\tif sts.IsRejected() {\n219: \t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n220: \t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n221: \t\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n222: \t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n223: \t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatus: framework.NewDefaultNodeToStatus(),\n224: \t\t\t\t},\n225: \t\t\t}\n226: \t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.NodeToStatus.Set(scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, sts)\n227: \t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.AddPluginStatus(sts)\n228: \t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, fwk.NewStatus(sts.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n229: \t\t}\n230: \t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, sts\n231: \t}\n232: \n233: \t// Run \"permit\" plugins.\n234: \trunPermitStatus := schedFramework.RunPermitPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n235: \tif !runPermitStatus.IsWait() && !runPermitStatus.IsSuccess() {\n236: \t\t// trigger un-reserve to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n237: \t\tschedFramework.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n238: \t\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n239: \t\t\tutilruntime.HandleErrorWithContext(ctx, forgetErr, \"Scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n240: \t\t}\n241: \n242: \t\tif runPermitStatus.IsRejected() {\n243: \t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n244: \t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n245: \t\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n246: \t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n247: \t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatus: framework.NewDefaultNodeToStatus(),\n248: \t\t\t\t},\n249: \t\t\t}\n250: \t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.NodeToStatus.Set(scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, runPermitStatus)\n251: \t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.AddPluginStatus(runPermitStatus)\n252: \t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, fwk.NewStatus(runPermitStatus.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n253: \t\t}\n254: \n255: \t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, runPermitStatus\n256: \t}\n257: \n258: \t// At the end of a successful scheduling cycle, pop and move up Pods if needed.\n259: \tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\n260: \t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Activate(logger, podsToActivate.Map)\n261: \t\t// Clear the entries after activation.\n262: \t\tpodsToActivate.Map = make(map[string]*v1.Pod)\n263: \t}\n264: \n265: \treturn scheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, nil\n266: }\n267: \n268: // bindingCycle tries to bind an assumed Pod.\n269: func (sched *Scheduler) bindingCycle(\n270: \tctx context.Context,\n271: \tstate fwk.CycleState,\n272: \tschedFramework framework.Framework,\n273: \tscheduleResult ScheduleResult,\n274: \tassumedPodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n275: \tstart time.Time,\n276: \tpodsToActivate *framework.PodsToActivate) *fwk.Status {\n277: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n278: \n279: \tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\n280: \n281: \tif sched.nominatedNodeNameForExpectationEnabled {\n282: \t\tpreFlightStatus := schedFramework.RunPreBindPreFlights(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n283: \t\tif preFlightStatus.Code() == fwk.Error ||\n284: \t\t\t// Unschedulable status is not supported in PreBindPreFlight and hence we regard it as an error.\n285: \t\t\tpreFlightStatus.IsRejected() {\n286: \t\t\treturn preFlightStatus\n287: \t\t}\n288: \t\tif preFlightStatus.IsSuccess() || schedFramework.WillWaitOnPermit(ctx, assumedPod) {\n289: \t\t\t// Add NominatedNodeName to tell the external components (e.g., the cluster autoscaler) that the pod is about to be bound to the node.\n290: \t\t\t// We only do this when any of WaitOnPermit or PreBind will work because otherwise the pod will be soon bound anyway.\n291: \t\t\tif err := updatePod(ctx, sched.client, schedFramework.APICacher(), assumedPod, nil, &fwk.NominatingInfo{\n292: \t\t\t\tNominatedNodeName: scheduleResult.SuggestedHost,\n293: \t\t\t\tNominatingMode:    fwk.ModeOverride,\n294: \t\t\t}); err != nil {\n295: \t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Failed to update the nominated node name in the binding cycle\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(assumedPod), \"nominatedNodeName\", scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n296: \t\t\t\t// We continue the processing because it's not critical enough to stop binding cycles here.\n297: \t\t\t}\n298: \t\t}\n299: \t}\n300: \n301: \t// Run \"permit\" plugins.\n302: \tif status := schedFramework.WaitOnPermit(ctx, assumedPod); !status.IsSuccess() {\n303: \t\tif status.IsRejected() {\n304: \t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n305: \t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n306: \t\t\t\tPod:         assumedPodInfo.Pod,\n307: \t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n308: \t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatus:         framework.NewDefaultNodeToStatus(),\n309: \t\t\t\t\tUnschedulablePlugins: sets.New(status.Plugin()),\n310: \t\t\t\t},\n311: \t\t\t}\n312: \t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.NodeToStatus.Set(scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, status)\n313: \t\t\treturn fwk.NewStatus(status.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n314: \t\t}\n315: \t\treturn status\n316: \t}\n317: \n318: \t// Any failures after this point cannot lead to the Pod being considered unschedulable.\n319: \t// We define the Pod as \"unschedulable\" only when Pods are rejected at specific extension points, and Permit is the last one in the scheduling/binding cycle.\n320: \t// If a Pod fails on PreBind or Bind, it should be moved to BackoffQ for retry.\n321: \t//\n322: \t// We can call Done() here because\n323: \t// we can free the cluster events stored in the scheduling queue sooner, which is worth for busy clusters memory consumption wise.\n324: \tsched.SchedulingQueue.Done(assumedPod.UID)\n325: \n326: \t// Run \"prebind\" plugins.\n327: \tif status := schedFramework.RunPreBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost); !status.IsSuccess() {\n328: \t\treturn status\n329: \t}\n330: \n331: \t// Run \"bind\" plugins.\n332: \tif status := sched.bind(ctx, schedFramework, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, state); !status.IsSuccess() {\n333: \t\treturn status\n334: \t}\n335: \n336: \t// Calculating nodeResourceString can be heavy. Avoid it if klog verbosity is below 2.\n337: \tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Successfully bound pod to node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(assumedPod), \"node\", scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, \"evaluatedNodes\", scheduleResult.EvaluatedNodes, \"feasibleNodes\", scheduleResult.FeasibleNodes)\n338: \tmetrics.PodScheduled(schedFramework.ProfileName(), metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n339: \tmetrics.PodSchedulingAttempts.Observe(float64(assumedPodInfo.Attempts))\n340: \tif assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp != nil {\n341: \t\tmetrics.PodSchedulingSLIDuration.WithLabelValues(getAttemptsLabel(assumedPodInfo)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(*assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp))\n342: \t}\n343: \t// Count pods scheduled after being flushed from unschedulablePods\n344: \tif assumedPodInfo.WasFlushedFromUnschedulable {\n345: \t\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"Pod scheduled after flush from unschedulablePods\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(assumedPodInfo.Pod), \"unschedulablePlugins\", assumedPodInfo.UnschedulablePlugins, \"pendingPlugins\", assumedPodInfo.PendingPlugins)\n346: \t\tmetrics.PodScheduledAfterFlush.Inc()\n347: \t}\n348: \t// Run \"postbind\" plugins.\n349: \tschedFramework.RunPostBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n350: \n351: \t// At the end of a successful binding cycle, move up Pods if needed.\n352: \tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\n353: \t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Activate(logger, podsToActivate.Map)\n354: \t\t// Unlike the logic in schedulingCycle(), we don't bother deleting the entries\n355: \t\t// as `podsToActivate.Map` is no longer consumed.\n356: \t}\n357: \n358: \treturn nil\n359: }\n360: \n361: func (sched *Scheduler) handleBindingCycleError(\n362: \tctx context.Context,\n363: \tstate fwk.CycleState,\n364: \tfwk framework.Framework,\n365: \tpodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n366: \tstart time.Time,\n367: \tscheduleResult ScheduleResult,\n368: \tstatus *fwk.Status) {\n369: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n370: \n371: \tassumedPod := podInfo.Pod\n372: \t// trigger un-reserve plugins to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n373: \tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n374: \tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n375: \t\tutilruntime.HandleErrorWithContext(ctx, forgetErr, \"scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n376: \t} else {\n377: \t\t// \"Forget\"ing an assumed Pod in binding cycle should be treated as a PodDelete event,\n378: \t\t// as the assumed Pod had occupied a certain amount of resources in scheduler cache.\n379: \t\t//\n380: \t\t// Avoid moving the assumed Pod itself as it's always Unschedulable.\n381: \t\t// It's intentional to \"defer\" this operation; otherwise MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue() would\n382: \t\t// add this event to in-flight events and thus move the assumed pod to backoffQ anyways if the plugins don't have appropriate QueueingHint.\n383: \t\tif status.IsRejected() {\n384: \t\t\tdefer sched.SchedulingQueue.MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue(logger, framework.EventAssignedPodDelete, assumedPod, nil, func(pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n385: \t\t\t\treturn assumedPod.UID != pod.UID\n386: \t\t\t})\n387: \t\t} else {\n388: \t\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue(logger, framework.EventAssignedPodDelete, assumedPod, nil, nil)\n389: \t\t}\n390: \t}\n391: \n392: \tsched.FailureHandler(ctx, fwk, podInfo, status, clearNominatedNode, start)\n393: }\n394: \n395: func (sched *Scheduler) frameworkForPod(pod *v1.Pod) (framework.Framework, error) {\n396: \tfwk, ok := sched.Profiles[pod.Spec.SchedulerName]\n397: \tif !ok {\n398: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"profile not found for scheduler name %q\", pod.Spec.SchedulerName)\n399: \t}\n400: \treturn fwk, nil\n401: }\n402: \n403: // skipPodSchedule returns true if we could skip scheduling the pod for specified cases.\n404: func (sched *Scheduler) skipPodSchedule(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n405: \t// Case 1: pod is being deleted.\n406: \tif pod.DeletionTimestamp != nil {\n407: \t\tfwk.EventRecorder().Eventf(pod, nil, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"FailedScheduling\", \"Scheduling\", \"skip schedule deleting pod: %v/%v\", pod.Namespace, pod.Name)\n408: \t\tklog.FromContext(ctx).V(3).Info(\"Skip schedule deleting pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n409: \t\treturn true\n410: \t}\n411: \n412: \t// Case 2: pod that has been assumed could be skipped.\n413: \t// An assumed pod can be added again to the scheduling queue if it got an update event\n414: \t// during its previous scheduling cycle but before getting assumed.\n415: \tisAssumed, err := sched.Cache.IsAssumedPod(pod)\n416: \tif err != nil {\n417: \t\tutilruntime.HandleErrorWithContext(ctx, err, \"Failed to check whether pod is assumed\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n418: \t\treturn false\n419: \t}\n420: \treturn isAssumed\n421: }\n422: \n423: // schedulePod tries to schedule the given pod to one of the nodes in the node list.\n424: // If it succeeds, it will return the name of the node.\n425: // If it fails, it will return a FitError with reasons.\n426: func (sched *Scheduler) schedulePod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state fwk.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) (result ScheduleResult, err error) {\n427: \ttrace := utiltrace.New(\"Scheduling\", utiltrace.Field{Key: \"namespace\", Value: pod.Namespace}, utiltrace.Field{Key: \"name\", Value: pod.Name})\n428: \tdefer trace.LogIfLong(100 * time.Millisecond)\n429: \tif err := sched.Cache.UpdateSnapshot(klog.FromContext(ctx), sched.nodeInfoSnapshot); err != nil {\n430: \t\treturn result, err\n431: \t}\n432: \ttrace.Step(\"Snapshotting scheduler cache and node infos done\")\n433: \n434: \tif sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes() == 0 {\n435: \t\treturn result, ErrNoNodesAvailable\n436: \t}\n437: \n438: \tfeasibleNodes, diagnosis, nodeHint, signature, err := sched.findNodesThatFitPod(ctx, fwk, state, pod)\n439: \tif err != nil {\n440: \t\treturn result, err\n441: \t}\n442: \ttrace.Step(\"Computing predicates done\")\n443: \n444: \tif len(feasibleNodes) == 0 {\n445: \t\treturn result, &framework.FitError{\n446: \t\t\tPod:         pod,\n447: \t\t\tNumAllNodes: sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes(),\n448: \t\t\tDiagnosis:   diagnosis,\n449: \t\t}\n450: \t}\n451: \n452: \t// When only one node after predicate, just use it.\n453: \tif len(feasibleNodes) == 1 {\n454: \t\tnode := feasibleNodes[0].Node().Name\n455: \t\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.OpportunisticBatching) {\n456: \t\t\tfwk.StoreScheduleResults(ctx, signature, nodeHint, node, nil, sched.CurrentCycle())\n457: \t\t}\n458: \t\treturn ScheduleResult{\n459: \t\t\tSuggestedHost:  node,\n460: \t\t\tEvaluatedNodes: 1 + diagnosis.NodeToStatus.Len(),\n461: \t\t\tFeasibleNodes:  1,\n462: \t\t}, nil\n463: \t}\n464: \n465: \tpriorityList, err := prioritizeNodes(ctx, sched.Extenders, fwk, state, pod, feasibleNodes)\n466: \tif err != nil {\n467: \t\treturn result, err\n468: \t}\n469: \n470: \tsortedPrioritizedNodes := newSortedNodeScores(priorityList)\n471: \tnode := sortedPrioritizedNodes.Pop()\n472: \ttrace.Step(\"Prioritizing done\")\n473: \n474: \tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.OpportunisticBatching) {\n475: \t\tfwk.StoreScheduleResults(ctx, signature, nodeHint, node, sortedPrioritizedNodes, sched.CurrentCycle())\n476: \t}\n477: \n478: \treturn ScheduleResult{\n479: \t\tSuggestedHost:  node,\n480: \t\tEvaluatedNodes: len(feasibleNodes) + diagnosis.NodeToStatus.Len(),\n481: \t\tFeasibleNodes:  len(feasibleNodes),\n482: \t}, err\n483: }\n484: \n485: // Filters the nodes to find the ones that fit the pod based on the framework\n486: // filter plugins and filter extenders.\n487: func (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatFitPod(ctx context.Context, schedFramework framework.Framework, state fwk.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) ([]fwk.NodeInfo, framework.Diagnosis, string, fwk.PodSignature, error) {\n488: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n489: \tdiagnosis := framework.Diagnosis{\n490: \t\tNodeToStatus: framework.NewDefaultNodeToStatus(),\n491: \t}\n492: \n493: \tallNodes, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NodeInfos().List()\n494: \tif err != nil {\n495: \t\treturn nil, diagnosis, \"\", nil, err\n496: \t}\n497: \t// Run \"prefilter\" plugins.\n498: \tpreRes, s, unscheduledPlugins := schedFramework.RunPreFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod)\n499: \tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins = unscheduledPlugins\n500: \tif !s.IsSuccess() {\n501: \t\tif !s.IsRejected() {\n502: \t\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, \"\", nil, s.AsError()\n503: \t\t}\n504: \t\t// All nodes in NodeToStatus will have the same status so that they can be handled in the preemption.\n505: \t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatus.SetAbsentNodesStatus(s)\n506: \n507: \t\t// Record the messages from PreFilter in Diagnosis.PreFilterMsg.\n508: \t\tmsg := s.Message()\n509: \t\tdiagnosis.PreFilterMsg = msg\n510: \t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PreFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n511: \t\tdiagnosis.AddPluginStatus(s)\n512: \t\treturn nil, diagnosis, \"\", nil, nil\n513: \t}\n514: \n515: \tvar nodeHint string\n516: \tvar signature fwk.PodSignature\n517: \tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.OpportunisticBatching) {\n518: \t\t// We get the node hint even if we have a nominated name for simplicity, but we could potentially avoid it\n519: \t\t// in this scenario in the future.\n520: \t\tnodeHint, signature = schedFramework.GetNodeHint(ctx, pod, state, sched.CurrentCycle())\n521: \t}\n522: \n523: \t// \"NominatedNodeName\" can potentially be set in a previous scheduling cycle as a result of preemption.\n524: \t// This node is likely the only candidate that will fit the pod, and hence we try it first before iterating over all nodes.\n525: \t// We take the same tack for hinted nodes from the batch module.\n526: \tif len(pod.Status.NominatedNodeName) > 0 || len(nodeHint) > 0 {\n527: \t\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.evaluateNominatedNode(ctx, pod, schedFramework, state, nodeHint, diagnosis)\n528: \t\tif err != nil {\n529: \t\t\tutilruntime.HandleErrorWithContext(ctx, err, \"Evaluation failed on nominated node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"node\", pod.Status.NominatedNodeName)\n530: \t\t}\n531: \t\t// Nominated node passes all the filters, scheduler is good to assign this node to the pod.\n532: \t\tif len(feasibleNodes) != 0 {\n533: \t\t\treturn feasibleNodes, diagnosis, nodeHint, signature, nil\n534: \t\t}\n535: \t}\n536: \n537: \tnodes := allNodes\n538: \tif !preRes.AllNodes() {\n539: \t\tnodes = make([]fwk.NodeInfo, 0, len(preRes.NodeNames))\n540: \t\tfor nodeName := range preRes.NodeNames {\n541: \t\t\t// PreRes may return nodeName(s) which do not exist; we verify\n542: \t\t\t// node exists in the Snapshot.\n543: \t\t\tif nodeInfo, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.Get(nodeName); err == nil {\n544: \t\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, nodeInfo)\n545: \t\t\t}\n546: \t\t}\n547: \t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatus.SetAbsentNodesStatus(fwk.NewStatus(fwk.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable, fmt.Sprintf(\"node(s) didn't satisfy plugin(s) %v\", sets.List(unscheduledPlugins))))\n548: \t}\n549: \tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, schedFramework, state, pod, &diagnosis, nodes)\n550: \t// always try to update the sched.nextStartNodeIndex regardless of whether an error has occurred\n551: \t// this is helpful to make sure that all the nodes have a chance to be searched\n552: \tprocessedNodes := len(feasibleNodes) + diagnosis.NodeToStatus.Len()\n553: \tsched.nextStartNodeIndex = (sched.nextStartNodeIndex + processedNodes) % len(allNodes)\n554: \tif err != nil {\n555: \t\treturn nil, diagnosis, nodeHint, signature, err\n556: \t}\n557: \n558: \tfeasibleNodesAfterExtender, err := findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatus)\n559: \tif err != nil {\n560: \t\treturn nil, diagnosis, nodeHint, signature, err\n561: \t}\n562: \tif len(feasibleNodesAfterExtender) != len(feasibleNodes) {\n563: \t\t// Extenders filtered out some nodes.\n564: \t\t//\n565: \t\t// Extender doesn't support any kind of requeueing feature like EnqueueExtensions in the scheduling framework.\n566: \t\t// When Extenders reject some Nodes and the pod ends up being unschedulable,\n567: \t\t// we put fwk.ExtenderName to pInfo.UnschedulablePlugins.\n568: \t\t// This Pod will be requeued from unschedulable pod pool to activeQ/backoffQ\n569: \t\t// by any kind of cluster events.\n570: \t\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/122019\n571: \t\tif diagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins == nil {\n572: \t\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins = sets.New[string]()\n573: \t\t}\n574: \t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins.Insert(framework.ExtenderName)\n575: \t}\n576: \n577: \treturn feasibleNodesAfterExtender, diagnosis, nodeHint, signature, nil\n578: }\n579: \n580: func (sched *Scheduler) evaluateNominatedNode(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod, schedFramework framework.Framework, state fwk.CycleState, nodeHint string, diagnosis framework.Diagnosis) ([]fwk.NodeInfo, error) {\n581: \t// In the future we could potentially use the hint if the nominated node failed.\n582: \t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/135163\n583: \tnnn :=
